<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">大君</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr">taikun</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:great.html>great</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prince.html>prince</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:title.html>title</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="Latn" lang="en">shōgun</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>Related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">taipan</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese"><a href = vnd.unilang:cantonese.html>Cantonese</a></a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="yue">大班</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yue-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">daai6 baan1</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> (28)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>Originally</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:accusative.html>accusative</a>/dative <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">iu</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*iwwiz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:west.html>West</a> Germanic <a href = vnd.unilang:variant.html>variant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*izwiz</i>, dative/<a href = vnd.unilang:accusative.html>accusative</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jūz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yū́</i>. Doublet <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a></i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:use.html>use</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> nominative stems <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:original.html>original</a> possessive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uwe.html>uwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:edelheid.html>edelheid</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:your.html>your</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nobility.html>nobility</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:your.html>your</a> gentility</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> shortened <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:e.html>E</a>.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:finally.html>finally</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i>.
